                      (function (config) {
                        function submitForm(event) {
                          if (event) {
                            event.preventDefault();
                          }
                          var form = document.querySelector('#brontoForm');
                          var successMessage = 'Thanks, we will be in touch!';
                          var currentDate = new Date();

                          var zipcode = document.getElementById('brontoFormZipcode');

                          form.innerHTML = successMessage;
                        }
                        window.brontoSubmit = submitForm;
                      })(window.ghsConfiguration);


                      // InAuth Configuration
                      (function (config) {
                        var inAuth = true;
                        window.localVariants = window.localVariants || {};
                        inAuth = window.localVariants['site.fraud.inAuth'];
                        if (!inAuth || !inAuth.selected) {
                          return;
                        }
                        setTimeout(function () {
                          var c = document.createElement('script');
                          c.type = 'text/javascript';
                          c.async = true;
                          c.src = 'https://' + config.inAuthCollectorUrl + '/cc.js?ts=' + (new Date()).getTime();

                          var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
                          s.parentNode.insertBefore(c, s);
                        }, 5000);
                      })(window.ghsConfiguration);

                      // initialize tracker for optimizely
                      if (window.optimizely && window.sessionStorage && !window.sessionStorage.getItem('optCheckForV2')) {
                        // track new site start
                        window.optimizely.push(['trackEvent', 'isV2']);
                        window.sessionStorage.setItem('optCheckForV2', 'true');
                      }


                      // Bounce Exchange
                      (function (config) {
                        if (!config.bounceExchangeEnabled) {
                          return;
                        }

                        setTimeout(function () {
                          var e = document.createElement('script');
                          e.src = 'https://tag.bounceexchange.com/' + config.bounceExchangeId + '/i.js';
                          e.async = true;
                          document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(e);
                        }, 3000);

                      })(window.ghsConfiguration);


                      // PerimeterX
                      (function (config) {
                        setTimeout(function () {
                          window._pxAppId = config.pxAppId;
                          // Custom parameters
                          // window._pxParam1 = "<param1>";
                          var p = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0],
                            s = document.createElement('script');
                          s.async = 1;
                          s.src = '//client.perimeterx.net/' + config.pxAppId + '/main.min.js';
                          p.parentNode.insertBefore(s, p);
                        }, 3000);

                      })(window.ghsConfiguration);
        </script>
